class="default">商品描述[39m[32m</h2>[39m[32m                                                                                                                                          	      <div id="productDescription" class="a-section a-spacing-small">                                                           <div class="disclaim">                                                                大小:[39m[32m<strong>[39m[32m480GB[39m[32m</strong>[39m[32m                                                                                &nbsp;|&nbsp;                           相机包款式:[39m[32m<strong>[39m[32mUltra II[39m[32m</strong>[39m[32m                                   [39m[32m</div>[39m[32m                                                   	                                                          	                         <!-- show up to 2 reviews by default -->                   	         	         		         			[39m[32m<p>[39m[32m480GB SDSSDHII-480G-G25 SSD II  SanDisk Ultra II SSD 480GBView larger  Give Your PC a Performance Boost The SanDisk Ultra II SSD is an easy and affordable way to upgrade and boost your PC's performance by up to 28 times (1). With this performance boost, you can enjoy no-wait boot up, shorter application load times, and quicker data transfer to make multi-tasking easy when it comes to work, entertainment, or both. In addition to cooler, quieter computing, the SanDisk Ultra II SSD adds up to 15% battery life to laptops and notebooks (2). From a global leader in flash memory storage solutions, the SanDisk Ultra II SSD can extend the life of your computer. Designed to Protect Your Data Housed in a durable aluminum case, the SanDisk Ultra II SSD has been engineered to resist shocks and vibrations, preserve the integrity of your data, and prevent data loss even if you drop your computer. And with S.M.A.R.T. (Self-Monitoring, Analysis, and Reporting Technology) capabilities, the drive monitors health and performance in real time to detect potential failures and help prevent data loss. Room for All Your Important Files The SanDisk Ultra II SSD offers a huge storage capacity of 480 GB (3) and is great for both home and business users. Use it to store all your important files, including graphics, media, images, documents, and the apps you use every day and still have room to spare.    28 times faster performance    Built for Speed and Endurance With performance up to 28 times faster than a typical hard drive (1), you spend less time waiting and more time working (or playing). The SanDisk Ultra II SSD delivers sustainable high performance, balancing super-fast read and write speeds with extended drive life. Thanks to a Mean Time Between Failures (MTBF) of 1.75 million hours (4), the SanDisk Ultra II can deliver years of fast, reliable performance, whether you're working with graphics-intensive applications or transferring big files at work.    Enhanced speeds    Ultra-Fast Speeds with nCache 2.0 Technology The SanDisk Ultra II SSD contains nCache 2.0 technology, which optimizes your computing experience by balancing all-out speed with long drive life. A large, non-volatile write cache consolidates small writes to boost random write performance and the long-term data endurance of the drive. This technology from SanDisk is designed to mediate how modern-day operating systems and flash memory interoperate. The result is ultra-fast response times and seamless multitasking even in the most resource-intensive applications.     This SSD monitors and provides updates on its health status.    Monitor the Health of Your SSD in Real Time Thanks to S. M. A. R. T. (Self-Monitoring, Analysis, and Reporting Technology) capabilities, this solid state drive can detect and report on various indicators of reliability and alert you of an impending drive failure while there is still time to take action.    Energy efficient design    Extends Battery Life Up to 15 Percent (2) Unlike traditional hard disk drives, the SanDisk Ultra II SSD has no moving parts so it runs cool and quiet even under heavy computing loads. This also means your PC uses less electricity and laptop battery life is extended up to 15 percent (2).     Multitask more efficiently    Efficient Multitasking Upgrading your computer with the SanDisk Ultra II SSD gives your machine the speed and power to keep up with all your computing activities. And it's easy to upgrade to the SSD yourself. The generous 480 GB (3) storage capacity means you will have room for all your important photos, videos, documents, and apps.        Legal Disclaimers (1) As compared to 7200 RPM SATA 2.5 inch hard drive. Based on published specifications and internal benchmarking tests using PCMark Vantage scores. (2) SanDisk SSD Deployment Whitepaper, 2013 (3) 1 gigabyte (GB) = 1,000,000,000 bytes. Some capacity not available for data storage. (4) Based on internal testing using Telcordia stress part testing. 				    	 					[39m[32m</p>[39m[32m
